  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d154846f-52db-465a-a877-c687ffb22c38'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText14235818421415094124" style="display:none">Despite her outgoing demeanor, Olivia is painfully insecure around the opposite sex—usually, she can’t get up the nerve to approach guys she’s interested in. But moving to Edinburgh has given her a new start, and, after she develops a crush on a sexy postgrad, she decides it’s time to push past her fears and go after what she wants.<br /><br />Nate Sawyer is a gorgeous player who never commits, but to his close friends, he’s as loyal as they come. So when Olivia turns to him with her relationship woes, he offers to instruct her in the art of flirting and to help her become more sexually confident.<br /><br />The friendly education in seduction soon grows into an intense and hot romance. But then Nate’s past and commitment issues rear their ugly heads, and Olivia is left brokenhearted. When Nate realizes he’s made the biggest mistake of his life, he will have to work harder than he ever has before to entice his best friend into falling back in love with him—or he may lose her forever….</span>

<div id="review_591048665" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591048665" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591048665?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591048665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2190176422052461442"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506553840i/24027716.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Before Jamaica Lane</i> is the third installment in the ODS series. I love Samantha Youngs writing, and with the exception of On Dublin Street, this is my favorite book of hers yet! It was a wonderful combination of funny, steamy, swoony, sweet and ansgty. A beautiful friends to lovers story!<br/><br/>Olivia has been to Scotland for a while now. She’s settling in. She has a job she loves as a librarian, her father, her ‘family’ which consists of Jo and Cole, and her friends. Nate has become one of her very be</span>
  <span id="freeText2190176422052461442" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506553840i/24027716.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Before Jamaica Lane</i> is the third installment in the ODS series. I love Samantha Youngs writing, and with the exception of On Dublin Street, this is my favorite book of hers yet! It was a wonderful combination of funny, steamy, swoony, sweet and ansgty. A beautiful friends to lovers story!<br><br>Olivia has been to Scotland for a while now. She’s settling in. She has a job she loves as a librarian, her father, her ‘family’ which consists of Jo and Cole, and her friends. Nate has become one of her very best friends. He’s attractive, he’s a sweet, and he’s a manwhore. Olivia is the exact opposite. Her experience in that department is very... er... limited. When she starts to develop a crush on a guy at the library, she asks Nate for advice.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“There’s a guy at the library. A student. Postgrad. I like him, but I sound like Rain Man every time I try to talk to him.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Olivia has an idea. She will get Nate to help, to tutor her. She wants to be good at sex. Who better to help her than the most experienced guy she knows? Nate is hesitant at first. He doesn’t want getting physical to change their friendship. As long as Olivia can agree to that, then he’s in. Let the lessons begin! <br><i>
  <blockquote>“So lets get this straight. You want me to fuck you in order to teach you how to fuck another guy?”</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506553840i/24027717.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of my favorite things about this book was the relationship between Olivia and Nate. There was an obvious connection there. They had passion, but they could always just hang out, watch movies, and talk. Liv was a never annoying, sweet, comical, feisty and fun heroine. She was so lovable. Then there was Nate. Nate appeared to be the super hot manwhore, but there was so much more to him than that. He was actually a little nerdy like Liv, he was understanding and had been through a lot. It’s made him the way he is. His heart it always in the right place.<br><br>Sex between friends... what could go wrong? After being with Nate, Olivia is finding herself thinking of her crush less and less. Not only are her lessons with Nate amazing, she feels like she has the whole package with him. She just wants him to feel the same. To love her, to want to be with her. Nate has things from his past. Things that hold him back from expressing the way he truly feels.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506553840i/24027715.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nate and Olivia have a lot of obstacles to overcome. Will they be able to continue their friendship with these feelings in the way? Will Nate ever be able to get over his past and return the feelings Olivia is so freely giving him? Olivia is not willing to settle for anything less than someone who can give them his all. Who wants her, loves her, needs her. She just hopes Nate is that someone for her. <br><br>Even though book one is my favorite of the series (duh... Braden!) Olivia and Nate are the best couple of the series! I adore them! They aren’t perfect, but they are perfect for one another. Friends to lovers stories are some of my favorites. Although they aren’t always the most original, I love the little twist this storyline brought to the original tale.   If you’re looking for a great story with a near perfect heroine, sexy and swoony hero, smoking hot chemistry, some mild tension and a few laugh out loud moments, you’ve found your book! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506553840i/24027718.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My favorite quote... ♥ ♥ ♥ </b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>“I never meant to fall in love with you. But I did. I felt it the first night I made love to you. I tried to walk away then because I’ve never felt so lost and yet so fucking found as I felt that night looking into your eyes as I moved inside you. I thought I should walk away…but I couldn’t stay away from you.”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_872507299" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/872507299" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/872507299?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780698149908" href="/book/show/25242308-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer872507299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer538749726633073223">This audiobook has been sitting on my shelf for at least a year. After being disappointed by the second book in this series, I figured that this series had lost it's luster for me. If it weren't for the fact that I've made it a personal mission to listen to all the books sitting on my Audible shelf, I probably would have continued to ignore this one. Lucky for me, I didn't. This story was fantastic!<br/><br/>'Before Jamaica Lane' tells the story of Olivia and Nate. Close friends, they never explored their</span>
  <span id="freeText538749726633073223" style="display:none">This audiobook has been sitting on my shelf for at least a year. After being disappointed by the second book in this series, I figured that this series had lost it's luster for me. If it weren't for the fact that I've made it a personal mission to listen to all the books sitting on my Audible shelf, I probably would have continued to ignore this one. Lucky for me, I didn't. This story was fantastic!<br /><br />'Before Jamaica Lane' tells the story of Olivia and Nate. Close friends, they never explored their attraction to one another. Their friendship was too valuable to risk.<br /><br />When Olivia finds herself crushing on a hot guy that frequents the library she works at, she is immediately overwhelmed by her own insecurities. With the exception of the disastrous night that she lost her virginity, she hasn't had sex with a man. In fact, she hasn't done much of anything sexual with other guys. Her youth was consumed by her mother's illness and grief over her death, not leaving time for normal teenage pursuits.<br /><br />Nate has spent the years since the loss of his first love sleeping with random women. He was the quintessential manwhore. With superstar looks, he didn't have to try hard to land a different woman in his bed anytime the mood struck. He kept it simple. Just sex. No emotions.<br /><br />Olivia approaches Nate with a proposal. She want to "practice", so that she can gain skills and confidence. Olivia wants to feel secure in her sexual prowess before she pursues her crush. If anyone can keep it "strictly sexual", she figures it's Nate.<br /><br />As I'm sure you can imagine, things between Nate and Olivia won't stay that simple. It isn't easy to keep emotions out of the sex, especially when the two have such a close relationship already. It doesn't take long for jealousy and love to become big factors.<br /><br />I loved the way Olivia and Nate's relationship evolved. This was a great friends to lovers storyline, with plenty of humor, drama and passion. It was a great story from start to finish.<br /><br /> I also appreciated the fact that Nate had to do some significant groveling after he screwed up. I hate it when an author lets the hero off with minimal effort or remorse after they seriously wrong the heroine. Maybe I'm bloodthirsty, but I expect them to pay! <br /><br />Overall, this was an excellent audiobook. The story was great, as was the narration. It wasn't overly complex, but had plenty going on to hold my interest. It was definitely better than the last book in this series, in my opinion. If you're looking for a friends to lovers story, this is a great choice.</span>
  <a data-text-id="538749726633073223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2331204670" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2331204670?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mel ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mel ☽" href="/user/show/41864935-mel">mel ☽</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=rereads">rereads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=grovelling">grovelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=favorite-heroes">favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=shy-dorky-heroines">shy-dorky-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=unrequited">unrequited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=ow-om">ow-om</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2331204670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6227220412615181146"><b>reread #idfk i reread this too many times</b> — <i>5 stars</i><br/><br/>this is my favorite friends to lovers book of <b>ALL. TIME.</b> also, this is the best book in the series imo. like, Joss and Braden who?? i can't think of any other friends to lovers books that would top this cuz this is s u p e r i o r. like the 5-star michelin steak, only the 1% can afford it kind of superior.<br/><br/>even though my reading taste has changed <i>a lot</i>, i still love this book and this is <u>my go-to reread if i read something with shitty grovelling</u> </span>
  <span id="freeText6227220412615181146" style="display:none"><b>reread #idfk i reread this too many times</b> — <i>5 stars</i><br><br>this is my favorite friends to lovers book of <b>ALL. TIME.</b> also, this is the best book in the series imo. like, Joss and Braden who?? i can't think of any other friends to lovers books that would top this cuz this is s u p e r i o r. like the 5-star michelin steak, only the 1% can afford it kind of superior.<br><br>even though my reading taste has changed <i>a lot</i>, i still love this book and this is <u>my go-to reread if i read something with shitty grovelling</u> or if the heroine forgives the hero after one grand gesture OR if the heroine has betraying body syndrome and gives in too easily or any of the other shit i hate. <br><br>but anyways, why is this my go-to reread you ask? well this has <b>THE BEST GROVELLING</b> i've ever read. hands down. why? because the heroine knows WHAT👏🏼SHE👏🏼DESERVES👏🏼 and she won't settle for less. whenever she doesn't forgive him and makes him work for it? i just tear up cuz i- i'm just so proud.<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590119970ra/29519602.gif" width="290" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>like, yes ma'am. please make the hero suffer some more thank you. <br><br>so here's what the book is about:<br><blockquote>↳ <b>Nate</b> (H) is a certified man ho who has a lot of experience, while <b>Liv</b> (h) has zero experience (she ain't a virgin tho). since Liv is insecure with her physical appearance and her lack of dating life and she's into this guy she sees at work, Nate offers to help her. after Nate gives a tutorial on how to flirt and how to kiss properly, their lessons turn sexual and well, y'all know how that goes.</blockquote><br><br>to be fair, i think <u>some might find the tropes here annoying</u> cuz Nate's introduction was kinda iffy since, again, he's the ho of the group and the heroine sees him flirting with someone he was about to take home. i don't know why i overlooked this the first time but now im just like<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590125377ra/29519750.gif" width="320" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>uhh... yeah. that wasn't fun. despite the fact that Nate was the man ho of the group, <b>this book has the least problematic/annoying OW drama out of all the books in the series</b>. even though he wasn't celibate after he met the heroine (this book is 7 months after the last book so that's how much they've known each other), we were spared from all that unlike other books in this series. <br><br>y'all don't believe me? <br><blockquote>↳ <b>Exhibit A:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2529357896?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">moonlight on nightingale way (#6)</a> <br>H and h are neighbors and H pulls a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15858248.Wallbanger__Cocktail___1_" title="Wallbanger (Cocktail, #1) by Alice Clayton" rel="nofollow noopener">wallbanger</a> move where he has sex every night and heroine hears him every. damn. night. h hears the same OW for 3 nights straight and H sleeps with this OW while h is already falling in love with him and vice versa.<br><br>↳ <b>Exhibit B:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140408-down-london-road" rel="nofollow noopener">down london road (#2)</a><br>H thinks of h while having sex with his girlfriend. oh, and there's cheating in this one.</blockquote><br>i could go on and on and on so yup. this book has the least annoying OW/OM drama.<br><br>also, <u>the heroine wasn't in love or pining after him</u>, in fact, she was more into the OM than the hero himself in the beginning. she does feel jealousy but it's not what you think. she feels jealous of Nate cuz it's so easy for him to "date" and talk to the opposite sex so i guess those are the silverlining. <br><br>as for Olivia, i actually didn't mind her insecurities. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"I don't want to be the person who looks in the mirror and hates what she sees, or be the person that moans about how she can't interact with a guy long enough to secure a date. That's not a good person to be, Nate."</b>
</blockquote><br>her personality, dorkiness and sarcastic sense of humor made me love her. also, imma be real here for a sec, i can relate to her insecurities cuz i can be shy when it comes to my dating life too soo it is what iss. the only thing i found annoying here was that <b>she needed Nate to validate the fact that she IS hot and sexy</b> but i guess that's part of the plot so whatever. <br><br>i actually really liked Nate. he's the type of guy who's goofy and nerdy but when it comes to the bedroom, he turns into this possessive dude that just left me<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590125054ra/29519743.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>I HAVE A WEAKNESS FOR NERDY HEROES OKAY? don't judge.<br><br>now let's get into the <b>grovelling</b>. the reason why Nate fucked up is because when Olivia was pouring her heart out and told him she loves him, he told her he'll never love her and walked away from her. Nate has baggage cuz he lost <b>Alana</b> (his first love) when he was young which then made him a man ho and have commitment problems so yes, this has <b>dead ex drama</b>. he even has a tattoo of OWs initial by his heart...<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576140359ra/28598315.gif" width="320" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>yikes i know. Olivia thinks she'll never be the love of his life and will forever be second best to his first love.<br><br>the grovelling here lasted a looong time and that's one of the reasons why i love this book. <u>Olivia never gave in until Nate proved she was the love of his life</u>, even though he already told her he loved her at one point. Nate is not the type of hero who gives the heroine space. nope. he's insistent as fuck. and ya know what? im glad he was cuz it SHOWS how much he was willing to fight for her. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"I never meant to fall in love with you. But I did. I felt it the first night I made love to you. I tried to walk away then because I've never felt so lost and yet so fucking found as i felt that night looking into your eyes as I moved inside you."</b>
</blockquote><br>i mean... <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590175245ra/29524341.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>i felt that. he does A LOT to prove his love for her and i honestly think this is the only book that left me 100% satisfied with the grovelling. <br><br>and btw, if y'all wanna know the <b>OW drama (SPOILERS)</b> here is the dead ex drama, 3 scenes of Olivia seeing Nate flirt with random women, and seeing him with this random OW after their break up but apparently he never did anything to her. as for <b>OM drama</b>, h kisses a random OM as part of her lesson, h goes on dates with OM after the breakup and OM is also the reason why the lessons started in the first place.<br><br>anyways, we need more books with grovelling scenes such as this one cuz im finding these lacking nowadays since apparently betraying body syndrome and H's being an asshole and makes the h work for it even though they're the ones who didn't do anything wrong is the trend nowadays. i can name plenty of books like this but just look at my 1-2 star rating for 2020 and if you know... YOU KNOW. <br><br>_______________________<br><br><b>original rating (march 2018)</b> — <i>5 stars</i></span>

<div id="review_1293086332" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1293086332" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1293086332?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-trust-feifei">i-trust-feifei</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=top-2015-reads">top-2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-recs">buddy-recs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=smartass-witty-banters">smartass-witty-banters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=fluffy-fluffer">fluffy-fluffer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=dirty-talker">dirty-talker</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1293086332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15716886914027989376"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432994623i/15034231.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“It occurred to me that more than loss, it was the longing that hurt the most.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>I can't remember the last time a book has made me feel the way I did after this one. It involves a) asking myself where has this book been all my life b) kicking myself very hard for not reading this sooner c) wanting to stay in this fictional world forever d) wishing that I could have this kind of all-consuming love in my life. <br/><br/>I've read <u>On Dublin Street</u> a year ago and while it still remains as one </span>
  <span id="freeText15716886914027989376" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432994623i/15034231.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“It occurred to me that more than loss, it was the longing that hurt the most.”</i>
</b><br><br>I can't remember the last time a book has made me feel the way I did after this one. It involves a) asking myself where has this book been all my life b) kicking myself very hard for not reading this sooner c) wanting to stay in this fictional world forever d) wishing that I could have this kind of all-consuming love in my life. <br><br>I've read <u>On Dublin Street</u> a year ago and while it still remains as one of my all-time favorite reads, I admit I've put off the series after reading mixed reviews for the 2nd book. But after all my lovely buddies insisted that I MUST read the 3rd instalment here and it could be read as a standalone, I finally caved in.<br><br>Let me just say that it was undoubtedly the best reading decision I've made in a while. Samantha Young puts out a story that not only transports her readers to the streets of Edinburgh but breathes life into this story by creating these completely endearing characters that you'll fall hard for. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Each book in the ODS series revolves around a couple and <u>Before Jamaica Lane</u> is <b>Nate &amp; Olivia's story</b>. Olivia moved to Scotland with her father after her mother's death while they were living in the States. During her stay here, she meets Nate who is Cam's best friend and they easily bonded sharing similar interests. Both of them are polar opposites with Olivia being the shy and inexperienced one at dating while Nate is the walking playboy of the city who can have any lady he wants.<br><br>When Olivia develops a crush on one of the guys in the library she works at, her lack of experience in the dating department had her pushing her luck by asking Nate for some advice. What started out as flirty lessons turned out to be something much more when the lines started to blur between friendship, lust and love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were just SO MANY things I loved about this read, honestly I'm flustered on even where to begin! <br><br>I can easily say that Olivia is one of the best heroines I've met and she's one of those women I can easily relate to, especially when it came down to her insecurities. She has a brilliant sense of humor with a touch of geek and above all, she has some major backbone. Her character growth was done so well that I swear she had me tearing up in a number of scenes, it made me feel so proud watching her firmly stand her ground. I was internally yelling "In your face, Nate!" when she didn't put up with Nate's bullshit anymore. In other words, she really owned her choices. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433003488i/15035792.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nate Sawyer &lt;- Oh yes adding him to my precious list of book boyfriends this instant. Although he was being portrayed as a walking manwhore in the beginning, the author did an amazing job by slowly peeling back the layers and revealed a much deeper and emotional side to this sexy man. There's a reason for his commitment-phobe issues and you can't even stay mad at him for long because you know deep down, he really cares for Olivia. He just needed time to work out his issues and it was easy for me to empathize with him after hearing his past. <br><br>Another thing I really loved about this book is Nate &amp; Olivia's connection right from the beginning. Their platonic relationship was fun to watch and had me chuckling at their geeky banters. Gradually it grew into something more when all the flirtatious and seduction lessons started and holy sex on a stick, the sexual tension was enough to burn down my reading device! Nate was absolutely divine in these scenes and if I was Olivia, I sure as hell wouldn't turn him down either. I need some Nate lovin' in my life!!<br><br>And then let's talk about that angst, I ABSOLUTELY LOVED IT. Nothing spells out angst better than the amount of grovelling done on Nate's part to get Olivia back in his life. Pretty sure my heart went through some massive workout during these scenes followed by me being in a blubbering mess of emotions that had me tearing up multiple times as both of them ripped apart their defenses and bear their hearts out. By the last stretch, I may have even cried harder because of how it was all tied up beautifully for this couple.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433001881i/15035519.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Samantha Young surely knows how to capture her readers' heart with her writing as I found myself consumed with Nate &amp; Olivia's love story from start till the end. Perfect balance of romance, steam, angst and humor; the author delivers a read that will sweep you off your feet with her storytelling. Fans of the friends to lovers trope will highly enjoy this one and definitely one of the best reads of this trope I've come across so far!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><u>Before Jamaica Lane</u> is the 3rd book in the On Dublin Street series and can be read as a standalone.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427351718i/14265304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15716886914027989376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=haha-funny">haha-funny</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer689907453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2516543807482847814"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424468344i/13765576._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I LOVE, LOVE, LOVE THIS BOOK!!!</b> It was fun, steamy, had a swoony, to-die for hero, a lovable heroine, and oh my god, the HUMOR!! I had a goofy grin on my face the entire time I read this gem of a story. Samantha Young’s writing is crazy addicting, and she combines just the right amount of angst, humor, and romance to create these passionate, all-consuming stories that hit the right spot. And I have to say, even though <u>On Dublin Street</u> will probably always be my favorite and have a spec</span>
  <span id="freeText2516543807482847814" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424468344i/13765576._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I LOVE, LOVE, LOVE THIS BOOK!!!</b> It was fun, steamy, had a swoony, to-die for hero, a lovable heroine, and oh my god, the HUMOR!! I had a goofy grin on my face the entire time I read this gem of a story. Samantha Young’s writing is crazy addicting, and she combines just the right amount of angst, humor, and romance to create these passionate, all-consuming stories that hit the right spot. And I have to say, even though <u>On Dublin Street</u> will probably always be my favorite and have a special spot in my heart, this book features the BEST couple – two characters who are so well-matched, well-rounded, and couldn’t be more perfect for each other. It’s truly a beautiful, romantic friends to lovers tale that had my heart RACING and fully invested in this story!<br><br>One thing this author absolutely excels at is creating irresistible, one-of-a-kind heroes I can’t help but fall in love with, and Nate Sawyer is no exception. He’s a manwhore – and he knows it well – but beneath that, he’s really such a good guy. Sweet, sensitive, caring and best friends with the heroine Olivia Holloway. They just get each other’s quirks and oddities.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424468344i/13765577._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Nate is self-confident, Olivia is the complete opposite – she’s shy (adorably so), and has fears and body-image insecurities I could really empathize with because I’ve been there myself. When she finally finds a guy she’s interested in, she enlists her best friend Nate’s help to learn to be more comfortable in her own skin. I have to mention that these were the scenes that made me SWOON. Hard. Witnessing Nate’s patience, understanding, and gentleness with the way he treated Olivia made my heart go pitter patter and want a Nate of my own.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424468344i/13765578._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The romance here was gradual and built up from the beginning. Of course, the attraction was there, but it was never acted on and Nate and Olivia were comfortable with being friends. Once those seduction lessons took place though, lines were blurred and feelings took place – deep, heartfelt emotions that neither of them realized existed until this point. In friends to lovers romances, I ADORE that self-realization where the characters come to an epiphany and see how much the other means to them...that final fall. And I have to say, the author nailed it in this book! So much swoon! ;)<br><br>Another aspect that was done really well in my opinion was the brilliant inclusion of all the other characters I’ve come to love since the start of the series. I think it’s a risky move because there’s always a chance these side characters will take up more book space than the main characters, but it worked well! Part of what shapes Nate and Olivia’s characters is their long-standing friendships with the others, and I’m glad they were part of their story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424468344i/13765579._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was surprised by the last 10% of the book, meaning I became a big baby and started crying because of how beautiful things were wrapping up. For me, that’s an indicator that this romance novel hit its mark, that things never got too cheesy or too angsty and drama-filled. Even though I tried to read this book as slow as possible to savor everything, I ended up finishing it in just hours. Sigh...this is one of very rare times I can say I genuinely adored EVERY. SINGLE. THING. about this book. And even though it’s only February, I already know this book will be one of my top favorites for this year, and how I wish I read it sooner!!<br><br><u>Before Jamaica Lane</u> is the 3rd book in the On Dublin Street series and can be read as a standalone. It’s been over a year since I last read anything from this series and when I picked this book up, I fell right into it. There is overlap with characters from the first two books, but I didn’t think it was so much they overshadowed the main couple.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2516543807482847814" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Obviously their agreement starts to change th</span>
  <span id="freeText18216951459552133340" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Seductive Stars!!</b><br><br>This starts when Olivia asks Nate to give her seduction lessons. <br>After all, Nate is a sexy-as-sin playboy who jumps from one-night-stand to another and Olivia is a shy girl that doesn’t know exactly how to connect with the opposite gender. <br>Since they are best-friends and geeks-soul-mates they believe that it will not going to interfere with their friendship. (Yeah, right.) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389399965i/8028481.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, since you all see where this is going, I’ll be short. Obviously their agreement starts to change things between them, their feelings also start to grow and somehow along the road they find out they aren’t just friends anymore. <br>And that’s will be when the problems begin, because Olivia’s insecurity’s and ghosts will set her back and Nate will also have a troubled path because reasons. (In the end, it always come down to their past. But you know that already.) <br>So in the end it comes down to this: How to you keep a person in your life after everything is changed and going back is no longer possible? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742019i/3117988.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love this series. My review could be resumed in just this sentence. <br>I loved Cam from the previous book, and Braden will always have a special place in my heart, but I think Nate just became my favorite. (It was probably his geek side! I felt connected :P ) Yeah, there was the times he annoyed me, but I loved him through basically the whole book. <br>And the best thing about this? MOST AWESOME HEROINE EVER! I think I have a book-crush on Olivia, she is one of the most amazing female MC that I’ve read. And I normally don’t like the girls <i>that</i> much.<br>Not to mention the whole gang is there, and it’s always great to read about them. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Not the most original one, but so well written that you quickly forget about that. Too much slow-paced in the beginning, dangerously close to boring, and that’s the only reason why I didn’t gave it 5 stars. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> amazingly written, as always. The Scottish expressions get me a little confused, but I can’t really judge that. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Loved both of them. I loved the fact that they’re both a little nerdy (not that usual) and had a pretty close friendship before their story began. Nate was a great MC and as I said before, Olivia was pretty much perfect. <br> <b>Steam: </b> So hot! Probably the hottest in the series so far. At least in my opinion.<br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="18216951459552133340" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1451044182" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1451044182" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1451044182?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1451044182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16898823718499009698"><b>5 **<u>manwhore miracle</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448814888i/17193294.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I didn't just want Nate to love me. I wanted him to love me the way I loved him. The kind of love that's so big it would last beyond a lifetime.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I promised myself I wouldn't review this book. Just some pressure free reading, but then the characters started to come off the page. And before I knew it I was in love with the story, made a little graphic and here I am writing a review. Oh well, stranger things have happened. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18115061-before-jamaica-lane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Before Jamaica Lane</a> is the third bo</span>
  <span id="freeText16898823718499009698" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>manwhore miracle</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448814888i/17193294.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I didn't just want Nate to love me. I wanted him to love me the way I loved him. The kind of love that's so big it would last beyond a lifetime.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I promised myself I wouldn't review this book. Just some pressure free reading, but then the characters started to come off the page. And before I knew it I was in love with the story, made a little graphic and here I am writing a review. Oh well, stranger things have happened. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18115061-before-jamaica-lane" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a> is the third book in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4167378.Samantha_Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Samantha Young</a>’s <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/90841-on-dublin-street" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street series</a> and just like all my friends predicted it was a complete win for me. After loving the first book and being slightly disappointed with the second I was reluctant to go back, but I can honestly say I don't regret picking this series up again. A complete win for me. <br><br>This is the story of Olivia and Nate, a friends to lovers contemporary romance, that will melt your heart, make you giggle like a little girl and fall madly in love with Nate in the meantime.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're not ready to hear this yet," he concluded. "But I do need you to know that I'm going to fight for you. I'm not making the mistake of walking away from you again. The only man in you future is me, Liv. The only kids in your future are mine.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Who are Nate and Olivia?<br><br>Both characters first appeared in the the second instalment <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140408-down-london-road" rel="nofollow noopener">Down London Road</a>. Nate is Cam's best friend and he works as a reviewer for video games and movies. And on top of that he is a manwhore with commitment issues. Just to put it out there, but don't hold it against him. He still needs to realise that his other best friend is the one.<br><br>Olivia is sort of a sister for Jo and only recently moved to Scotland with her dad. She is a librarian and the 'other best friend' who will eventually be madly in love with Nate.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448815045ra/17193298.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Olivia</b> is simply adorable. A quirky, sharp witted gal with an interesting sense of humour, who is incapable to form a single coherent thought when faced with men she is attracted to. <b>Nate</b> is a charmer, warm hearted, a nerd and probably the best friend any girl can have. Romantic interest or not. <br><br>I have to say, I love both main characters on their own. Nate and Liv are wonderful, but when they come together magic happens. They click as friends right from the start and rather quickly become inseparable. They have amazing banter and complete each other. But things get really interesting when Liv falls for a guy at work and asks Nate to help her become more confident. Those lessons may or may not turn out different than what she would have thought.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It occurred to me that more than loss, it was the longing that hurt the most.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What can I say? Ms. Young created a lovable story about two friends who belong together. The chemistry and connection is undeniable and really captured my attention. The writing is smooth and effortless. The family aspect with all the surrounding characters makes this a well rounded and highly enjoyable read. Not to mention an explosive one when Nate and Liv get into their lessons. Holy hotness batman. And you know it can't all be smooth sailing, right? There are a lot of people involved that could get hurt and things in their past might turn this little game into a powder keg. But that's where the fun begins.<br><br>Well, I am convinced to keep going with the series. There are after all some very interesting and still single friends and family member left on the streets of Edinburgh...;D<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_588658402" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588658402" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588658402?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11757728-geri-reads?shelf=all-my-loves">all-my-loves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588658402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9825131242281727111"><b>5 stars!!</b><br/><br/><b>WARNING: This review may contain slight spoilers and copious amount of sentences starting with "I loved..."</b><br/><br/>I've always been a sucker for books with a friends-to-lovers theme and Before Jamaica Lane is one of the better ones out in the sea of books with similar tropes. Yes, the recurring themes in this book has been done a number of times but what set this apart from other books is the connection and the chemistry between the two main characters. <br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=307uv54' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389284711i/8015029.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>We met Olivia and Nate during Cam and</span>
  <span id="freeText9825131242281727111" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!</b><br><br><b>WARNING: This review may contain slight spoilers and copious amount of sentences starting with "I loved..."</b><br><br>I've always been a sucker for books with a friends-to-lovers theme and Before Jamaica Lane is one of the better ones out in the sea of books with similar tropes. Yes, the recurring themes in this book has been done a number of times but what set this apart from other books is the connection and the chemistry between the two main characters. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=307uv54" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389284711i/8015029.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We met Olivia and Nate during Cam and Jo's story in Down London Road. Olivia moved to Scotland with her father after she lost her job there. Nate was one of Cam's bestfriend. He's gorgeous, fun and is a total commitment-phobe. They started off as friends, bonded by their love for movies, books, etc. <br><br>There was already an attraction there especially on Olivia's part. But she's painfully shy around guys and a little bit insecure because of her inexperience. Plus, she never thought that Nate might see her that way. So she buried that flicker of attraction and moved on. <br><br>Nate doesn't do commitment. It sounds like a tired old cliche but he has a pretty good reason (at least in his head) for it. Nate had already met the love of his life but she died and Nate's heart died along with her. So he flirts with everything that moves and doesn't make any promises. But Olivia was different. She was the first female that he feels comfortable with. He can actually be himself around her.<br><br>Then someone caught Olivia's eye but being painfully shy especially around guys, she doesn't quite know how to deal with it. Enter Nate, the manwhore best friend who's going to teach her how to get the guy. They find themselves spending more and more time together and things started escalating from there. And boy, did it escalate. Their first kiss...wow!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=xp1y81" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389284711ra/8015030.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Samantha Young had me emotionally invested in both Olivia and Nate. They are, by far my favorite couple in this series. (Sorry Ellie and Adam) I loved how their relationship developed and the transition between friends to lovers doesn't feel rushed or contrived. <br><br>The author really took her time to develop these characters. I understood why Olivia was insecure. I hate it when heroines are insecure for no apparent reason whatsoever but Olivia's insecurity didn't annoy me. They endeared her to me. Same with Nate's reluctance to enter into any relationship. I did want to slap him upside in the head a couple of times but he's a guy. Making stupid decisions in relation to matters of the heart is a given, so I wasn't too upset with him.<br><br>I loved their conversations and their "Would you rather" game. Olivia is hilarious. She's the best heroine evah. She's a librarian, a little geeky with a wonderful sense of humor. She fits Nate perfectly. And I can totally see why Nate could totally fall for her. I usually hate it when a hot guy goes gaga for a girl and I'm left confused as to why he likes her in the first place. But here, I TOTALLY GET IT!!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=nly05t" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389454273ra/8031762.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Of course, this wouldn't be a Samantha Young book without some angst. But don't worry it's not that bad like On Dublin Street. (READ: NOT THE JOSS-INDUCED KIND OF ANGST) But still pretty angsty if may say so myself. I especially love the groveling in this book. I totally understood why Olivia didn't immediately forgive him. No one wants to feel like they're the second choice. I loved that Olivia wanted it all and she wasn't willing to settle for second place. I must say Nate more than proved himself, so I was totally happy when how everything turned out.<br><br>We also get to catch up with the gang in this book. Some parts of this book actually overlaps Castle Hill. And while I still like Braden, Joss really annoyed me. She has gotten progressively abrasive and annoying in this series. Ugh! (What does Braden see in her again?) <br><br>Anyway, I still loved this one very much. I'll definitely recommend it to everyone who love these types of stories. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/wR0uo9Z" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389454273ra/8031763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="9825131242281727111" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_839845204" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/839845204" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/839845204?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=angsty-intense">angsty-intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=library-checkout">library-checkout</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer839845204" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8146922372921841141"><i> Reread May 2020: still holds up </i><br/><br/><b> **5 stars!** </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “You'll end up living a lonely life if you're waiting around for perfect.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/bjl.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416382987i/11946100.png' alt=' photo bjl.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So, it's no secret that I absolutely <i> adore </i> Samantha Young's books. There seems to be the perfect balance of angst, happy, and emotional in her writing formula that just works for me as a reader. Ever since I read On Dublin Street, I've been not so subtlety shoving her books down my friends' throats for them to read.<br/><br/>Before Jamaica Lane is the story of library assistan</span>
  <span id="freeText8146922372921841141" style="display:none"><i> Reread May 2020: still holds up </i><br><br><b> **5 stars!** </b><br><br><b> <i> “You'll end up living a lonely life if you're waiting around for perfect.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/bjl.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416382987i/11946100.png" alt=" photo bjl.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, it's no secret that I absolutely <i> adore </i> Samantha Young's books. There seems to be the perfect balance of angst, happy, and emotional in her writing formula that just works for me as a reader. Ever since I read On Dublin Street, I've been not so subtlety shoving her books down my friends' throats for them to read.<br><br>Before Jamaica Lane is the story of library assistant, Olivia and her best guy friend Nate, who embark on a series of flirting lessons in order for Olivia to gain more confidence around the other sex. We've heard this story before, right? WRONG! Ms. Young did a wonderful job with an old story line and making it into something uniquely her own. <br><br><b> <i> “I want to be someone's big love, Dad. I think I deserve to have the man I love love me back just as much.” </i> </b><br><br>Olivia is a heroine to stand by; she's loyal to her friends and family, not quick to judge anyone, and very endearingly hopeless when it comes to men (at the beginning of the book at least). I loved the development of her character throughout the book from a semi-meek girl, into a woman who finally accepts herself for what she is: a confident, attractive and smart woman with a lot to offer. <br><br>I'm not one for dual perspectives, but I really did find myself wishing as a reader that we could see Nate's point of view, as he could be so hard to read sometimes. And here is a segment from the main summary of the book as proof that I'm not spoiling anything, <i> "But then Nate’s past and commitment issues rear their ugly heads, and Olivia is left broken-hearted." </i> Even without the summary giving this away, it was fairly obvious that Nate had many issues due to his tragic past and he would end up hurting Olivia. The scene in which this happens had me in knots and I felt like I was going to puke (not really, but you know what I mean). I kept returning to it as I continued reading because I felt I gained more insight to the story. So if only for that scene alone, I bow down to Ms. Young. You like to play with reader's heartstrings like they're a bloody violin. Bravo!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Most authors neglect to have the party at fault grovel enough to make up for past wrongs. Nate more than made up for it to Olivia, and in return Olivia didn't give into Nate so easily, thank god. One of my favorite quotes from the book:<br><br><b> <i> "I thought I could do it. I thought I could lie to the both of us. But seeing you on the street last week with that guy and the little girl... It was a glimpse into the future. It didn't hit me until right in that moment that walking away from you, from us, meant having to watch you be with someone else, have kids with someone else... Christ Liv, I couldn't breathe." </i> </b>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>One thing that stood out to me in this book and On Dublin Street was how well Ms. Young wrote as an American. I am convinced that she's lived in the states, despite being from the UK because she does such a wonderful job writing as an American that it's believable in the books. I know what you're thinking, there aren't that many differences between Americans and the Scottish, but it's the small things that make up one's culture. Like how Olivia calls shotgun and the Scots have no idea what she meant. Plus the American slang/idioms used throughout the entire book. Masterfully done.<br><br><b> <i> “I didn't just want Nate to love me. I wanted him to love me the way I loved him. The kind of love that's so big it would last beyond a lifetime.” </i> </b><br><br>So now that I'm done gushing over Ms. Young and her book, I highly recommend this series to anyone. This book technically could be read out of order, but I wouldn't recommend it. Start with the first book and make your way down. Plus, I am extremely excited for the next book about Hannah and Marco, an intriguing romance that began to develop in Down London Road.<br><br><b> <i> “I never meant to fall in love with you. But I did. I felt it the first night I made love to you. I tried to walk away then because I've never felt so lost and yet so fucking found as I felt that night.” </i> </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8146922372921841141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer815487658" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17925901265202901890"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Before Jamaica Lane<br/><b>Series:</b> On Dublin Street #3<br/><b>Author:</b> Samantha Young<br/><b>Release Date: </b> January 7th, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Samantha Young once again done a very well job. I can only congratulate her writing this wonderful mix of fluffy, fuzzy emotions, angst, hot sex and heartwarming romance. Before Jamaica Lane is a cute story that I highly recommend to every fan of ‘best friends to lovers’ kind of stories. Why? Because it made me laugh, </span>
  <span id="freeText17925901265202901890" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Before Jamaica Lane<br><b>Series:</b> On Dublin Street #3<br><b>Author:</b> Samantha Young<br><b>Release Date: </b> January 7th, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Samantha Young once again done a very well job. I can only congratulate her writing this wonderful mix of fluffy, fuzzy emotions, angst, hot sex and heartwarming romance. Before Jamaica Lane is a cute story that I highly recommend to every fan of ‘best friends to lovers’ kind of stories. Why? Because it made me laugh, swoon, melt, throw myself on the floor, pick myself from it and then once again roll of the bed. And even if my back hurt a little bit because of that, my fluttering heart made up for it. Twice. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389214121i/8006438.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before Jamaica Lane had everything a good new adult read has to have: hot romance, panty melting hero, relatable heroine, adorable storyline, awesome dialogues and making you laugh out loud sense of humor. <br><br>Before Jamaica Lane tells story of Olivia. She’s been only few months in Scotland and almost from the beginning she formed deep bond with Nate. They fell into best friends category very quickly. Olivia is curvy and being as inexperienced as she was made her very self-conscious. So when the hot ‘I can have sex with every woman in this city’ Nate promised her to tutor her in Eros’ ways Olivia said yes. Plain and simple. But when between librarian Liv and Panty dropping Mr Fuck me senseless tutoring in flirting turned into lessons between the sheets, things started to change..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389214121i/8006439.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia was fabulous heroine. I felt her so much. Not only did she suffer from the problems which seemed similar to mine’s, which made me relate with her on another level, she also took everything with smile and witty, snarky comments even if inside she was blubbering mess. I admired her for that. I found Liv’s inside voice great. She was funny, so darn cute and she was a geeky librarian! What’s more to need? <br><br>Nate was another story altogether. I liked him, I really did. He was a geek (score!), he was a very sexy, drool worthy Love Teacher (can I get a tutor like him too? I really need one.) and he made me feel all kind of bothered! What’s more my heart easily ached for him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389214121i/8006440.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Together they were the bomb! The funniest, most adorable on geeky level couple I’ve ever read about. They were a match made in heaven. Swoon!<br><br>Samantha Young used every trick she had up her sleeve and she did it wisely. Fans of On Dublin Street series should feel extremely satisfied with what she came up with. I definitely was. Not only did I have a great time, while reconnecting with the gang, I also glimpsed into lives of Nate and Olivia and fell in love with both of them. Perfect read for those who crave some lightness and romantic tale of love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389214121i/8006441.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956727i/7492465._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1240264327?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>,
