        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1240264327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13145452754587787192"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428086092r/14362555.jpg?v=1428086095615' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>Lines were being blurred, and other lines were actually being crossed. There were a whole lot of lines and none of them were of a solid consistency.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420501766ra/13233126.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I only have one question after finishing this book: WHERE HAS THIS BEEN ALL MY LIFE?! I have no idea why I didn't continue with this series after reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_' title='On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young' rel='nofollow noopener'>On Dublin Street</a> when it just came out. I'll blame my mile long TBR. But after hearing all about Nate from gushing GR friends, I figured it was way past time we get introduced. </span>
  <span id="freeText13145452754587787192" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428086092r/14362555.jpg?v=1428086095615" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Lines were being blurred, and other lines were actually being crossed. There were a whole lot of lines and none of them were of a solid consistency.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420501766ra/13233126.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I only have one question after finishing this book: WHERE HAS THIS BEEN ALL MY LIFE?! I have no idea why I didn't continue with this series after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street</a> when it just came out. I'll blame my mile long TBR. But after hearing all about Nate from gushing GR friends, I figured it was way past time we get introduced. I was a little bit hesitant starting this since I read On Dublin Street such a long time ago, I remember a sum total of nothing from it. Oh and I kinda sorta mighta skipped book 2. (What? I'm a rebel like that) But I digress. My fear was since I couldn't remember any of the secondary characters introduced in ODS that I'd feel lost jumping straight into book 3. And while it took a bit for me to get everyone straight, I never did find myself confused. I was totally enraptured in this wonderful book in just a few paragraphs.<br><br>Olivia, even though she's not my preferred type of heroine, was easily one of my favorite characters I've read in a while. She's so quirky in her nerdiness that her insecurities never bothered me. As a matter of fact, I found absolutely everything about her endearing, <b>especially</b> her insecurities. After losing her mother to cancer, Olivia moved to live with her father in Scotland. Having been taking care of her ailing mother, Olivia never really had a chance to experience the things that most teenagers do; going on dates, fooling around. So despite her outgoing and quirky personality, the second she's around a guy she's attracted to, she gets shy and absolutely tongue-tied. Meeting Nate when she first moved to Scotland, she would have been just as shy around him, had he not immediately put her directly in the friend zone. Now they're the best of friends. So who else can Liv come to to help her get over her shyness with men so that she can catch the eye of a super cute graduate student she meets in the Library where she works?<br><br>Nate is the biggest manwhore of the group. His gorgeous looks and charismatic personality guarantee that never spends the night alone. But Liv gets something that the women don't get... his true self. So when she comes to him for help, he knows that he'll help her. If the constant zing of attraction that runs between them is any indication, it certainly won't be a chore either.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Liv?" his brows creased. "Just say it."<br>It rushed out in a burst of geek. "It's size is a little problematic because despite my tendency to ramble, my mouth is pretty small and it won't all fit in it and I have a gag reflex that might be a problem so I don't know how-"<br>"Liv-" Nate was choking on laughter. "Take a deep breath."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>OK...so maybe it won't be all serious either.<br><br>I have to say how much I loved Liv and her personality. Her nerdy sayings, her and Nate's movie nights and "would you rather" games were so adorable. I honestly couldn't get enough of it. Also, it's so refreshing to read about a shy and awkward with the opposite sex girl that <b>isn't</b> a virgin. And despite her insecurites, Liv was anything but weak. This is a woman that had no fear speaking her mind and standing up for what she wants and is right.<br><br>Then there was the electric connection between her and Nate that only continued to get hotter and hotter with each new "lesson"<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">God...Nate..."<br>"That's right, babe...<br>I'm taking you straight to heaven."<br>"Heaven. Hell," I panted, my fingers raking the wall. "Who cares as long as I ride there on an orgasm."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428122057ra/14371412.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nate is not the simple manwhore that he appears. Having had an experience in his teenage years that have forever put him off of love, he has reasons for his sleeping around. And for once in my reading history, I thought they were ones that make sense. Nate was just this perfect combination of sexy and adorable. The way that he's with Liv makes you completely fall in love with him. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Does this feel like I don't want you?"<br>I reared against him, silently begging for more. "No." I shook my head, and then arched back as he thrust into me. Just like that, Nate began to screw the mortification right out of me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There was also the sex. Did I mention the sex? Because oh my god, the sex.<br><br>Even though you know right away where these lessons will lead, it was still fun as hell watching both Liv and Nate fall for each other. Liv being strong and accepting of it, while Nate? Not so much. I wanted to throttle him for the way he handles everything. And then I wanted to hug Liv for not being the pushover that she could have been and standing up for herself...no matter how stubborn she may have been about it later. This was one of the best grovels I've read in a long time. It was, in a word, perfection.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">You're not ready to hear this yet," he concluded. "But I do need you to know that I'm going to fight for you. I'm not making the mistake of walking away from you again. The only man in your future is me, Liv. The only kids in your future are mine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>If you're a fan of the friends to lovers trope, this book is simply a must read. Don't be an idiot like me and keep pushing off reading it. Drop whatever you're doing right now, and read it immediately. Trust me. You won't be sorry.<br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414533288i/11664451._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13145452754587787192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/816086666?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=manwhore">manwhore</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer816086666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer460687018654364960"><b>4.5 Stars<br/><br/><i>"You have next to no experience and I have too much.”<br/>My mouth twisted with annoyance. “It’s not really a good time to brag about that shit, Nathaniel.”<br/>He grinned at me. “I’m not bragging. I’m helping.”<br/>“Helping?”<br/>“Helping you.”<br/>“Helping me how?”<br/>“Helping you get laid.”</i></b><br/><br/>That’s it Nate. Take one for the team! Olivia and Nathaniel have been best friends for nine months, ever since meeting through the rest of the Dublin Street crowd. Olivia’s been insanely attracted to Nate from the beginning, b</span>
  <span id="freeText460687018654364960" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars<br /><br /><i>"You have next to no experience and I have too much.”<br />My mouth twisted with annoyance. “It’s not really a good time to brag about that shit, Nathaniel.”<br />He grinned at me. “I’m not bragging. I’m helping.”<br />“Helping?”<br />“Helping you.”<br />“Helping me how?”<br />“Helping you get laid.”</i></b><br /><br />That’s it Nate. Take one for the team! Olivia and Nathaniel have been best friends for nine months, ever since meeting through the rest of the Dublin Street crowd. Olivia’s been insanely attracted to Nate from the beginning, but with her self confidence level hovering somewhere near ankle level there’s no way she’ll ever try for anything more than friendship. Add to the fact the Nate is a practicing manwhore who’s vowed never to commit and you have a relationship slotted firmly in the friend zone. Not that this was a real problem for Olivia or Nate. These two genuinely enjoyed their friendship and the time they spent hanging out together with no promise of sex. Until the thought of sex entered the equation.<br /><br />Though Olivia’s ruled out the idea of pursuing anything with Nate, a girl still feels the need for a little somethin somethin every now and then and poor Liv with her stunted sexual history would rather not feel like a socially awkward freak every time she tries to interact with the penis carrying half of the population. So when our gal Liv finds herself attracted to a big, hot piece of man trying to get his education on at the library she works at, she knows she has to make some changes if she ever hopes to come into contact with a living, breathing cock again. It only takes Liv getting fall on your face drunk and some embarrassing confessions about her sexual history and our man Nate’s on board to help his bestie learn to let loose and become the confident sex kitten she’s meant to be.<br /><br />So at this point I was reminding myself that this was one of the oldest tropes around and of course they’d develop feelings for each other. You know what? I didn’t give a shit. The story was that cute and melt-your-panties right off of you hot that it didn’t even faze me. When these two finally got together, I could actually FEEL the heat and attraction that had been simmering between them for months. It stopped being a story about hot piece Nate helping Olivia discover her sexy and all about Nate and Olivia enjoying the hell out of each other’s sexy. From the first time they hooked up and every time after, the bond between Liv and Nate was an undeniable force, even though Nate’s told Olivia over and over theirs isn’t a relationship that can ever be anything more than friendship because he lost his first love to cancer and that’s it for him. He’s only got one go ‘round in him. What’s a newly sexed up and in love girl to do when she realizes she may not get the guy?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”But my girl deserves more than whatever you two are up to. You deserve to start making a life with someone. You deserve to be the love of some man’s life.”</i>
</b><br /><br />It’s obvious the road to happily ever after is not going to be an easy one for these two, but it was absolutely a believable and satisfying one. I loved Olivia and how she knew her worth and stood her ground. I loved Nate realizing almost immediately he’d fucked up and fucked up royally. Seeing Nate own up to his mistakes and Liv grow as a confident person and stand her ground made the entire book worth the read.<br /><br />I kept going back and forth between a 4 and 5 star rating for this but it comes down to the fact that I keep reading this book over again between other books or during downtime. If I’m going to keep re-reading it after only one week, I think it warrants the big 5 Stars from me.</span>

<div id="review_821346243" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/821346243" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/821346243?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer821346243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4601650767524366668"><b>FIVE PERFECT STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"One simple lesson in seduction between two friends can turn into so much more." </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459159._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I loved everything, and I mean everything about this perfectly romantic novel. I've been told over and over again that I would love this story, and to those of you who knew me enough well of course you were completely correct. I didn't want this book to ever end. This story came complete with the perfect heroine, an outrageously gorgeous hero and a story line that left me weak at the knees, br</span>
  <span id="freeText4601650767524366668" style="display:none"><b>FIVE PERFECT STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"One simple lesson in seduction between two friends can turn into so much more." </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459159._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved everything, and I mean everything about this perfectly romantic novel. I've been told over and over again that I would love this story, and to those of you who knew me enough well of course you were completely correct. I didn't want this book to ever end. This story came complete with the perfect heroine, an outrageously gorgeous hero and a story line that left me weak at the knees, bravo Samantha young you've written the most perfect novel and my favourite in the series so far. Here are my 'I fell in love hard' dreamy book thoughts ...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459161._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Olivia has no shortage of great friends, a job that she loves and security living in a city that she has started to call home. What she doesn't have is a whole lot of confidence when it comes to matters of the heart so when her gorgeous best friend, Nate Sawyer agrees to give her some lessons in the art of seduction Olivia jumps at the chance. Olivia knows that nothing will develop between them, Nate likes the ladies a little too much and never promises to commit and Olivia has a bad case of insecurity which means she believes someone like Nate would never fall for her. Olivia and Nate have firmly landed themselves into the friend zone but when attraction starts to develop into something more they have to make the decision to fight for something real or allow broken hearts, insecurities and bad decisions get in the way of what could be a loving forever, together.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459160._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400alt=" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>This novel showcased Samantha young at her very best, I felt butterflies in my tummy at every romantic filled page and conversation, so much so that I felt like I never wanted to say goodbye to this book. The characters were marvellous, move over every book boyfriend that I've ever fallen for and make room for my favourite heroine to date, Olivia was everything that I like in a female character, she was relatable, funny, sweet, gorgeous and had enough back bone to make me cheer for her from page one right to the end. Unusually for me Olivia as the heroine was the shining star in this novel but that's not to say that I didn't enjoy this books commitment-phobe, the delectable Nate Sawyer. I loved his friendship with Olivia and I adored how he made her feel special and loved. Everything about their connection was super duper lovey-dovey and I can gladly say that this couple have won the spot for most favourite couple of the series. As for the story itself well I can't deny that I go ga-ga over a friends to 'lets-tear-up-those-sheets-together-baby' story. The narrative was engaging as well as entertaining and as crazy as it sounds I feel such a fondness for these characters and their developing friendships as the series continues. Samantha Young has created a series that I'd be sad to say goodbye to but I'm hoping she already realises that readers will continue to love her characters and novels, I for one will continue to be a firm fan and I'd be happy to be left to re-read this gorgeous story over and over again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459162._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>It's no secret that I'm a little infatuated with authors who truly know how to write romance stories, especially those than make readers fall in love right alongside the characters. Samantha Young is an author who never fails to make me smile, swoon and get swept up in her delicious story telling. Olivia and Nate are a couple that I'll love to re read over and over again and I can't imagine ever forgetting about this loveable novel. This is the third instalment in the 'On Dublin Street' series and for me most definitely stands out as a favourite. If you love a well put together romance story with plenty of friendship, steam, moments of fun and an added bit of angst then you must not miss out. Go grab it readers, enjoy ... Kisses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391801353i/8459163._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4601650767524366668" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588669635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5832247687190390565">Nate and Olivia are best friends but can their friendship survive being lovers as well?<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Olivia...I think we can all relate to her in one way or another. I loved her humor and especially her growth. <br/><br/>• Nate...Wow, he really won me over. I liked him before but I guess I never caught on to how yummy he is! His growth was a little harder to read.<br/><br/>• The lessons...OMG, where was my Nate when I needed him? Scratch that...all girls need a Nate! <br/><br/>• Olivia's lingerie.<br/><br/>• Liv and Nate's banter...love</span>
  <span id="freeText5832247687190390565" style="display:none">Nate and Olivia are best friends but can their friendship survive being lovers as well?<br><br><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Olivia...I think we can all relate to her in one way or another. I loved her humor and especially her growth. <br><br>• Nate...Wow, he really won me over. I liked him before but I guess I never caught on to how yummy he is! His growth was a little harder to read.<br><br>• The lessons...OMG, where was my Nate when I needed him? Scratch that...all girls need a Nate! <br><br>• Olivia's lingerie.<br><br>• Liv and Nate's banter...loved the "Would You Rather."<br><br>• The letters/notes.<br><br>• The dirty talk!<br><br>• The Gang! <div id="review_591049350" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591049350" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591049350?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591049350" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12174688361847115222">4.5 Stars<br/><b><br/>Before Jamaica Lane</b> is a best-friends-that-turn-into-something more type of romance, albeit, VERY reluctantly and with some heartache along the way. This was such an addictive read I read it in one day, but I can’t say I’m surprised with this story coming from one of my favorite romance authors: Samantha Young. <br/><br/>Olivia has moved to Scotland with her father for a fresh start and to be closer to her father’s sort of adopted daughter, Jo. Olivia is ready for the move after caring for her mo</span>
  <span id="freeText12174688361847115222" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><b><br />Before Jamaica Lane</b> is a best-friends-that-turn-into-something more type of romance, albeit, VERY reluctantly and with some heartache along the way. This was such an addictive read I read it in one day, but I can’t say I’m surprised with this story coming from one of my favorite romance authors: Samantha Young. <br /><br />Olivia has moved to Scotland with her father for a fresh start and to be closer to her father’s sort of adopted daughter, Jo. Olivia is ready for the move after caring for her mother through a bout with cancer and then ultimately losing her in the battle. Because of putting her mother first, Olivia basically skipped over those years fumbling through romances, so even though she’s in her mid 20s, she has next to no experience with the opposite sex, and is extremely shy. Therefore, when anyone seems to be interested, Olivia invariably mucks up her chances. This is with the exception of Nate. He’s gorgeous, and pretty much a man-whore, but for some reason she immediately clicked with him upon arriving in Scotland, bonding over all things geek. That doesn’t mean she’s immune to Nate’s charm and charisma. Olivia’s pretty much a goner and harbors the crush of all crushes for him, but because romance doesn’t seem possible, she’s comfortable with him and they become best friends. She tries to turn off the hurt and jealousy that comes whenever he snags a girl to take home, which is OFTEN! <br /><br />Nate has no problem with the opposite sex. He’s the king of the one-night stand after having a very painful experience in love very early on. When Olivia asks Nate to help her overcome her crippling shyness with men, he agrees, but makes it clear he doesn’t want any confusion on his position: <br /><b><br />“You trust me to do this with you, but I’ve got to trust that you won’t try to make this into anything more than a friend helping out another friend.”</b><br /><br />And I want to smack Nate again after reading that quote! <br /><br />Soon their “lessons” turn into so much more (big surprise) and before they know it Olivia and Nate are in over their heads. Olivia figures this out pretty early on, but can’t stop because her heart is too far gone. Oh, Olivia! Nate on the other hand is very stubborn and I wanted to slap him upside the head more than a few times! And this is where the angst comes in. Samantha Young has a talent for incorporating just enough drama and angst to puncture your heart, and keep you hooked without drawing it out to the point of frustrating you and turning you off the story. Don’t let me turn you off of Nate, though, he had good reasons and he was a sweetheart helping Olivia see her value and desirability:<br /><b><br />Nate said quietly, “Liv’s perfect. She deserves perfect. She won’t be settling for anything less.”</b><br /><br />See, sweatheart.<br /><br />Nate and Olivia were so very hot together! Ms. Young writes some of the hottest scenes and this story is no exception. She builds things up, and up, and up, until the sexual tension makes you ready to combust! <br /><br />As if this lovely romance wasn’t enough we get updates on our favorite past couples: Joss and Braden, Jo and Camden, and Ellie and Adam. Fans will recognize the events of this story overlap with the events in Castle Hill, the Joss and Braden novella and we get a little of what happened through Olivia’s perspective. I must mention that I love the whole “family” feeling you get with all the characters. Olivia was accepted into this big group almost like a surrogate sister. All the girls were in her corner when she needed them the most. I adored Olivia’s father Mick, as well. Every girl needs a father like him. <br /><br />Favorite Quote: (Spoilery)<b><br />“I never meant to fall in love with you. But I did. I felt it the first night I made love to you. I tried to walk away then because I’ve never felt so lost and yet so fucking found as I felt that night looking into your eyes as I moved inside you. I thought I should walk away…but I couldn’t stay away from you.”</b><br /><i><br />A copy was provided by NAL in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12174688361847115222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1737849830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1399298299897464855"><b> 4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I liked this one. I like the friends-to-more type stories, and this didn't disappoint. I was frustrated with the H, but he made up for it in the end with some good grovel -- which I've found is necessary for me to like a character again. We all make mistakes and have our own baggage we bring into relationships, but I think it is crucial that we acknowledge our mistakes and grow from them. I feel like both of these characters did that, and they ended up being better indi</span>
  <span id="freeText1399298299897464855" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I liked this one. I like the friends-to-more type stories, and this didn't disappoint. I was frustrated with the H, but he made up for it in the end with some good grovel -- which I've found is necessary for me to like a character again. We all make mistakes and have our own baggage we bring into relationships, but I think it is crucial that we acknowledge our mistakes and grow from them. I feel like both of these characters did that, and they ended up being better individuals together. I loved their "would you rather" questions, especially in the epilogue ;)<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Olivia and Nate's story. They meet with mutual friends, and become best-friends right away by bonding over their geekiness. They both have an underlying attraction, but value their friendship enough to not cross the line. Olivia gets drunk one night, and confesses her insecurities and struggles with men because she is inexperienced. She ends up propositioning Nate to tutor her in the art of dating and sex, because Nate is a well known manwhore. Lines get crossed and stronger feelings develop, but they have some big obstacles to get over before they figure out that they're meant to be...but they do get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Olivia's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They were friends before they developed stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Nate. I liked him. I understood why he pushed away, but I appreciated how he worked hard to get the h back.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Olivia. I had some issue with her and her insecurities at first, but I ended up liking her in the end.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b> Low/moderate. I teared up a few times, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H does a good bit of hot/cold behavior because he is scared and his last relationship died of cancer. Both the h and H push away and pursue at times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They don't become intimate until about halfway through, but they have some hot chemistry and scenes once they do.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. Birth control and std status are mentioned. The H states that he had never gone without condoms before, but I don't remember any mention of what happened with the h's one other sexual experience.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is an OM that the h had been crushing on that comes around when the h and H are separated. The H is seen with OW during the separation (he later says nothing happened between them). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a separation of maybe a few months (?) between them, and the H says that he hadn't been with any OW after the h. There is no suggestion or mention that the h was with anyone else either.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Loss of a parent and girlfriend to cancer, and H was manwhore before h. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had a cute jump ahead epilogue and as close to a HEA as you can get being a HFN <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the h is pregnant and they get engaged <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I'm sure many will be fine with this ending and call it a HEA, but for consistency purposes -- I'm going to call it a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it on loan through my local library.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd say that this should be <u>Safe</u> for most readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the H and h pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a HEA ending, but I'm sure it's probably close enough for most <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer741571372" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15589934600065030783"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Wow Samantha Young has a fantastic sense of humor! This book had fun banter, one <b>HOT</b> couple, and a terrific group of great friends. What a good read! <br/><br/>Olivia was a lovable heroine who I found to be very relatable. I <b>LOVED</b> her sense of humor, her insecurities and her courage to ask for <b>MORE</b>!!<br/><br/>Nate and Olivia have a terrific friendship and these two would be a perfect couple…<br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Nate, your commitment phobia is showing again." He turned to me in mock horror. <br/><br/>"Where</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText15589934600065030783" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Wow Samantha Young has a fantastic sense of humor! This book had fun banter, one <b>HOT</b> couple, and a terrific group of great friends. What a good read! <br><br>Olivia was a lovable heroine who I found to be very relatable. I <b>LOVED</b> her sense of humor, her insecurities and her courage to ask for <b>MORE</b>!!<br><br>Nate and Olivia have a terrific friendship and these two would be a perfect couple…<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>"Nate, your commitment phobia is showing again." He turned to me in mock horror. <br><br>"Where?" He patted his cheeks anxiously. "Get it off me."</i>
</b><br><br>This story gets all sorts of sexy when Olivia asks for “lessons” from her bff, Nate…<br><br><b>
  <i>"I want you...I want you to teach me how to be...good at sex."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>"We'll start tonight."</i>
</b><br><br>In true friends to lovers fashion Nate and Olivia hit some snags along the road...<br><br><b>
  <i>"I want a love like what my dad had with my mom. I want want Joss and Braden have. Jo and Cam. Ellie and Adam." The tears flowed freely before I could stop them. "You already had that with Alana."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491936617ra/22464462.gif" width="325" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nate and Olivia were downright perfect together and the ride although predictable was nonetheless enjoyable!<br><br><b>
  <i>"...the 'after' we'd found together...well...it was forever."</i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15589934600065030783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer831375190" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2971247167174550231"><u>The<b> On Dublin Street series </b> has been all over the place for my star ratings:</u><br/> <br/><b>»On Dublin Street</b> was definitely 	★	★	★	★	★. I loved that book.<br/><b>»Down London Road</b> was ★	★. I felt bored through the majority of the book.<br/><b>»Before Jamaica Lane</b> is ★	★	★. <br/><br/>I spent the first 19% of the book trying to keep tracking of all the characters. It felt like <u>character chaos</u>. I made cliff notes (see below) so I could refer to them as I was reading. I suppose that is expected when you read book 1 in 2012, book 2 in 201</span>
  <span id="freeText2971247167174550231" style="display:none"><u>The<b> On Dublin Street series </b> has been all over the place for my star ratings:</u><br> <br><b>»On Dublin Street</b> was definitely 	★	★	★	★	★. I loved that book.<br><b>»Down London Road</b> was ★	★. I felt bored through the majority of the book.<br><b>»Before Jamaica Lane</b> is ★	★	★. <br><br>I spent the first 19% of the book trying to keep tracking of all the characters. It felt like <u>character chaos</u>. I made cliff notes (see below) so I could refer to them as I was reading. I suppose that is expected when you read book 1 in 2012, book 2 in 2013 and now book 3 in 2014. <br><br>Once the story started just focusing on <b>Olivia</b> and <b>Nate</b> it flowed better and was easier to follow. I never got fully immersed in their love story because all the old gang with their issues kept popping up in the story.<br><br>I am intrigued by book 4 and 5 because I want to see how Ms. Young does Hannah and Cole's books. So, I may continue on. <br><br>***********************************************<br><b>Cliff notes </b>for me to keep the characters straight while I read this one.<br><br>Book 1 - Jocelyn/Joss &amp; Braden<br>Book 1.5 - Ellie (Braden's sister) &amp; Adam (Braden's best friend)<br>Book 2 - Johanna/Jo (waitress where Joss worked) &amp; Cameron/Cam (bartender where she works)<br>Book 3 - Olivia/Liv (librarian and &amp; Nate (Cam's friend)<br>Cole - Jo's younger brother<br>Olivia's dad - longtime friend of Jo's dad (in prison)<br>Clark &amp; Eloide - parents to Hannah &amp; Declan<br>Mick - Liv's dad<br>***********************************************<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358249908s/15760001.jpg" alt="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140408.Down_London_Road__On_Dublin_Street___2_" title="Down London Road (On Dublin Street, #2) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363128044s/16140408.jpg" alt="Down London Road (On Dublin Street, #2) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17766752.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371745197s/17766752.jpg" alt="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18746504.Fall_from_India_Place__On_Dublin_Street___4_" title="Fall from India Place (On Dublin Street, #4) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1384254640s/18746504.jpg" alt="Fall from India Place (On Dublin Street, #4) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20617402.Untitled__On_Dublin_Street__5_" title="Untitled (On Dublin Street #5) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png" alt="Untitled (On Dublin Street #5) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Continuing story where secondary characters from the first book become the main focus in subsequent books. <br>Book 1 - Jocelyn &amp; Braden | Book 2 - Johanna &amp; Cameron | Book 3 - Olivia &amp; Nate | Book 4 - Hannah &amp; Marco | Book 5 - Cole &amp; ?<br><br><i>Novellas:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16897452.An_On_Dublin_Street_Christmas__On_Dublin_Street___1_1_" title="An On Dublin Street Christmas (On Dublin Street, #1.1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1375445206s/16897452.jpg" alt="An On Dublin Street Christmas (On Dublin Street, #1.1) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363894173s/17665083.jpg" alt="Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.5) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18621172.Castle_Hill__On_Dublin_Street___2_5_" title="Castle Hill (On Dublin Street, #2.5) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_701255549" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/701255549" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/701255549?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer701255549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1605867082876886712"><a href='http://imgur.com/RBOXEuD' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389123071i/7992265._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>I loved On Dublin Street, it was a six star read for me, so I was pretty excited for Down London Road. So, I was pretty shocked on how disappointed I was with Down London Road, considering how much I loved book 1. Now, it’s Before Jamaica Lane and I really, had no expectations.<br/><br/>Before Jamaica Lane is pretty much an adorable read, from start to finish. Samantha Young is getting back to her roots and I think she’s writing more romance than angst, and I’m very grateful for that. Although </span>
  <span id="freeText1605867082876886712" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/RBOXEuD" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389123071i/7992265._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>I loved On Dublin Street, it was a six star read for me, so I was pretty excited for Down London Road. So, I was pretty shocked on how disappointed I was with Down London Road, considering how much I loved book 1. Now, it’s Before Jamaica Lane and I really, had no expectations.<br><br>Before Jamaica Lane is pretty much an adorable read, from start to finish. Samantha Young is getting back to her roots and I think she’s writing more romance than angst, and I’m very grateful for that. Although Jamaica Lane was not quite as good as Down London Road, I definitely like the direction Young is taking the series.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/WrzoLga" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389123071i/7992266.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Olivia and Nate are best friends. Olivia is very reserved and doesn’t have a lot of experience with sex, she’s awkward, she doesn’t know how to flirt and she wants to date. Nate is a major man-whore with a bunch of issues. Olivia proposes an idea to Nate. Olivia wants Nate to teach her how to flirt and land her crush. As Nate “teaches” Olivia in the art of seduction, Olivia is finding it hard to separate her growing feelings from Nate.<br><br>Cute story line right? I liked Nate and I liked Olivia. The beginning was a bit slow, but there’s plenty of character development. You get a general idea of who Olivia is and yes it’s kind of hard to believe a twenty-something gal that inept in the world of dating, but it’s a book, so I go along with the story line. Olivia could be only as describe as SUPER CUTE. She’s smart, successful and pretty much the “average looking” girl (despite the cover model).<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/b1AwMC0" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389123071i/7992267.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nate is gorgeous, flirty, charismatic man whore we all girls love. I liked Nate overall, he’s no Braden, but Nate did play the sexy guy with pent-up-issues very well. Yes, the other characters from the previous books are sprinkled in throughout. I am not sure if I cared for those parts, I think at some point, there can be too many characters and it was difficult for me to keep track of who was who. Overall, the banter between Olivia and Nate was cute. Nate was a bit possessive and arrogant, which I enjoyed.<br><br>There wasn’t anything completely wrong with Jamaica Lane, it just wasn’t a Dublin Street homerun. If you want a sweet read with a little bit of tension in the mix, then Jamaica Lane is for you.<br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>More reviews here - &gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/</a><br><br><b>Series Order<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358249908s/15760001.jpg" alt="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> | <a rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17665083.Until_Fountain_Bridge__On_Dublin_Street___1_5_" title="Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.5) by <div id="review_1154971993" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1154971993" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1154971993?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1154971993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6963006728296104451">The Dublin Street books are one of my favorites book of all time! I connected at such a deep level with all the characters and loved spending my time with them. I managed to enter their big family and soon I felt part of them, without ever wanting to leave.<br/>Samantha Young did a great job in creating such great and strong heroes, that surely leave a mark on her readers. <br/><br/>In "Before Jamaica Lane" we get to read the story of Liv, Jo's sister and Nate, Cam's best friend. Since the second book, we got </span>
  <span id="freeText6963006728296104451" style="display:none">The Dublin Street books are one of my favorites book of all time! I connected at such a deep level with all the characters and loved spending my time with them. I managed to enter their big family and soon I felt part of them, without ever wanting to leave.<br>Samantha Young did a great job in creating such great and strong heroes, that surely leave a mark on her readers. <br><br>In "Before Jamaica Lane" we get to read the story of Liv, Jo's sister and Nate, Cam's best friend. Since the second book, we got a glimpse of their relationship and find that they are close friends, spending a lot of time together. I simply love friends that turn into something more. There is something about this kind of connection that surpasses the instant love element. When you are a true friend, you understand all of that person's aspects and accept his pros and cons without judging. I consider that relationship being complete, having a natural path, from loving that person's soul to loving and enjoying their exterior.<br><br>As for the heroes, Olivia was a very sweet and lovely character to follow. I kind of connected with her better that with Nate, because in a way I could see a lot of her features in me. Olivia is also very shy, has a passion for books and wants to make a change, to be more confident and to express her feeling more openly. Her greatest fear is being confident with her body and managing to attract men. Having around a best friend that oozes confidence helps a lot, because Olivia asks Nate to teach her how to be seductive and sexy. After Nate agrees, they soon embark in a thrilling ride, full of lust, sex, passion and in the end, love. <br><br>I loved the way their relationship developed, from being friends to passionate lovers. The love scenes were amazing, hot and made you want so much more. You could see how good they are together and wanted them to soon realize it as well. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475662389i/20747446.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Thanks to Nate, Olivia changed so much, not only in her body confidence but as a person. She became stronger and more aware of her priorities and desires. In relationship with Nate she wanted to be the only one, to be cherished, to fully trust his love for her. She believed in the ONE and I swoon as well over that idea, of loving someone for life. <br><br><b> <i> " This may sound selfish and childish, but it’s how I feel. I want to be the love of someone’s life. I can’t be second best. And I definitely can’t be second best for you. I can’t spend the rest of my life loving a man who can’t love me back in the same way. " </i> </b><br><br>Although she wanted Nate to teach her how to be sexually confident, she realized that love means so much more, and was not going to have only a half of it. She wanted all, and I was so in love with her for this thing.<br>Nate on the other hand, had some demons of his own, losing his great love at the age of 18. We could now understand why the man whore attitude and the lack of commitment from his side. He didn't want to go through that again and his heart was out of any relationship. Until he met Olivia, of course and his barriers began to fall one by one. I liked Nate so much when he realized what Olivia means to him, his speech was one of the most romantic lines I've ever read. <br><br><b> <i> " I always thought that I kept a distance from women because I knew I’d never be able to love someone the way I loved her. I was wrong. I kept my distance because I was afraid of finding the kind of love my parents have, and I was afraid of what it would do to me if I lost that kind of love. I never meant to fall in love with you. But I did. " </i> </b><br><br>I liked how tender, gentle and romantic he could be.He changed her, making her more confident and aware of her qualities, and Olivia changed his life forever, she gave him her heart and never let go.<br><br><b> <i> "I want you all the time, Olivia. The past few weeks have been torture without you. And despite what you might still think, I promise there has been no one else. How could there ever be?"</i> </b> <br><br>I enjoyed seeing all the characters from the previous book together, they have a special place in my heart and all the books from this series are unique and with a strong story behind them.<br>Second to Cole, Nate is my favorite, because although all the mistakes he made, he fought hard to get Olivia back, and I enjoyed every second of it. He had the love of his life right under his nose and just couldn't figure it out in the beginning. Once realizing it, you will love the person he's become. <br><br>5 stars!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="6963006728296104451" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12909810603662892489">Loved it. I don't write long reviews for contemporary books, and especially NA, simply because I never have much to say but I will highlight: <b>THE FEELS.</b> I am extremely picky with tropes and I DNF or dislike most NA books I read (some I never even bother to put on GR because I DNF within first three chapters) and this one was perfect. Best friend Nate (love that name!) helps the MC become confident enough to ask out this guy/get his notice by teaching her things. The way the romance was portrayed</span>
  <span id="freeText12909810603662892489" style="display:none">Loved it. I don't write long reviews for contemporary books, and especially NA, simply because I never have much to say but I will highlight: <b>THE FEELS.</b> I am extremely picky with tropes and I DNF or dislike most NA books I read (some I never even bother to put on GR because I DNF within first three chapters) and this one was perfect. Best friend Nate (love that name!) helps the MC become confident enough to ask out this guy/get his notice by teaching her things. The way the romance was portrayed was perfect for me. No cheese, just good stuff. I will definitely check out the author's other work.<br /><br />Side note: forgot who rec'd this book to me when I asked for a good NA rec, whoever it is I. OWE. YOU. This is my favorite NA book I've read.</span>

The friends-to-lover and learning-seduction troupes are my favorites!</b> What could go wrong? I think the language may have hindered me from enjoying what could have been a good story. I don't care for 1-POV past tense. I really missed Nate's perspective. But worse than that, <b>it was written in tell-not-show mood</b>. The author wrote stuff like "I felt so attracted" instead of writing about the actually feeling. <b>I don't want to <i>know</i>, I want to <i>feel</i></b>. And this book enticed no other feelings than boredom from my part. <br><br>I might go over this review in the future. Right now, I just want to move on to a great book. <b>There was good stuff, but for me, it sadly didn't work out. Obviously, I'm in a minority here so just because I didn't love it doesn't mean that you won't. </b><br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/899402903?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=finished-series">finished-series</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer899402903" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer254275683071137854"><b>December 2016 Re-Read:</b><br/>I think whoever uploads digital content for my local library has been on vacation because the selection of new content is just sad. What to do, what to do. Re-reading tried and true favorites was my solution. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18115061.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_' title='Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young' rel='nofollow noopener'>Before Jamaica Lane</a> was the first to come to mind. It's just as good as the two other times I've read it ♥<br/><br/><b>March 2015 Re-Read:</b><br/>So a week or so ago I was in a reading slump and decided to re-read one of my personal favorites, which just happens to be the first in this ser</span>
  <span id="freeText254275683071137854" style="display:none"><b>December 2016 Re-Read:</b><br />I think whoever uploads digital content for my local library has been on vacation because the selection of new content is just sad. What to do, what to do. Re-reading tried and true favorites was my solution. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18115061.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a> was the first to come to mind. It's just as good as the two other times I've read it ♥<br /><br /><b>March 2015 Re-Read:</b><br />So a week or so ago I was in a reading slump and decided to re-read one of my personal favorites, which just happens to be the first in this series: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street</a>. It did the trick and I've been flying high with mostly 4 and 5-star reads since. It just felt good to read something I knew I was going going to love. An equal favorite in this series is this one, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18115061.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a>. Nate and Liv's chemistry is off the freakin' charts and I wanted to re-experience their story just for the hell of it...and I'm so glad I did ♥<br /><br /><b>Original Review from June 2014:</b><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17766752.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a> is the third installment in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4167378.Samantha_Young" title="Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Samantha Young</a>'s On Dublin Street series. When I read the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street</a>, it blew me away. The other books <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17665083.Until_Fountain_Bridge__On_Dublin_Street___1_5_" title="Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.5) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Until Fountain Bridge</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140408.Down_London_Road__On_Dublin_Street___2_" title="Down London Road (On Dublin Street, #2) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Down London Road</a> were also very good but not as good in my opinion, but this book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17766752.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a> shoots right back up there to amazing. Don't get me wrong, Joss and Braden remain my absolute favorite characters in this series but now Liv and Nate come in a close second. Liv and Nate have been best buds for about a year- a male/female platonic relationship that they both enjoy. Liv can hang with the guys but she can't seem to interact with a man she's romantically interested in due to her lack of confidence in her sexuality. Nate has plenty of sexual confidence and experience. Who better to teach Liv how to be confident in this department than her best friend? As the story progresses, the reader really gets to know Liv and Nate's characters, along with their personal histories that have shaped them into their present-day selves. The storyline in this book is pretty predictable, which usually annoys me, but in this book I just didn't care. Liv and Nate are so sexy and amazing together I couldn't put this book down! One thing I enjoy about this series as a whole is in each book that comes out, the reader gets to catch up with the couples that were featured in previous books. That said, there is an important development in Joss and Braden's relationship that you won't want to miss in this book! I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17766752.Before_Jamaica_Lane__On_Dublin_Street___3_" title="Before Jamaica Lane (On Dublin Street, #3) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Before Jamaica Lane</a> and I would highly recommend it to fans of the On Dublin Street series.<br /><br /><b>My favorite quote:</b><br /><i>"It was possible that men, actual men, not adolescent boys and young college boys, might find me attractive-might actually be ok with a woman who was a little overweight, had curves and an ass on her. And here I'd thought Sir Mix-A-Lot wrote "I Like Big Butts' just because it was catchy."<br /></i><br /><br />The On Dublin Street series includes the following installments as of June 2014:<br />#1-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street</a><br />#1.1-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16897452.An_On_Dublin_Street_Christmas__On_Dublin_Street___1_1_" title="An On Dublin Street Christmas (On Dublin Street, #1.1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">An On Dublin Street Christmas</a><br />#1.5-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17665083.Until_Fountain_Bridge__On_Dublin_Street___1_5_" title="Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.5) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Until Fountain Bridge</a><br />#2-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16140408.Down_London_Road__On_Dublin_Street___2_" title="Down London Road (On Dublin Street, #2) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Down London <div id="review_589068968" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/589068968" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/589068968?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17766752-before-jamaica-lane">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>,
